BCU PO DE DAG LA SOGS PA 'OD ZER GRANGS MED

BDE BA DANG PHRAD PAR BRTZON ZHING BDAG GI BDE BA LHUR LEN PA'I
SEMS CAN

SKYO BAR BYA BA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS MNGON PAR
'BYUNG BA DANG, KHAMS GSUM PA THAMS CAD LAS 'BYUNG BA'I SNGON GYI
LTAS YANG DAG PAR BSTAN PA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB

SEMS DPA' RNAMS MNGON PAR 'BYUNG BA DANG, RANG LA RAG LAS PAR
SPYOD CING, GZHAN GYI DRING MI 'JOG PA LA BRTEN PA'I PHYIR, BYANG
CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS MNGON PAR 'BYUNG

BA DANG, DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA'I STOBS BCU DANG, MI BSNYENGS PA THOB
PA DANG MTHUN PAR YANG DAG PAR BSTAN PA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS
DPA' RNAMS MNGON PAR 'BYUNG BA DANG, KYE

RGYAL BA'I SRAS, CHOS NYID KYIS KYANG BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' SRID
PA'I THA MA PA NI GDON MI ZA BAR MNGON PAR 'BYUNG STE, KYE RGYAL
BA'I SRAS, BCU PO DE DAG NI, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'

RNAMS SEMS CAN 'DUL BA'I DBANG GI PHYIR, ,MNGON PAR 'BYUNG BA
YONGS SU STON PA DAG GO, KYE RGYAL BA'I SRAS, BCU PO 'DI DAG NI,
BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS KYI DKA' BA

SPYOD PA'I SBYOR BA STE, BCU GANG ZHE NA, 'DI LTAR DMA' BA LA MOS
PA'I SEMS CAN GYI KHAMS YONGS SU SMIN PAR BYA BA'I PHYIR, BYANG
CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS DKA' BA SPYOD PA STON


@369A *, ,PA DANG, LTA BA'I RNAM PA LA GNAS PA'I SEMS CAN RNAMS
GYEN DU BSKYOD PA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS DKA' BA
SPYOD PA STON PA DANG, LAS DANG BYA

BAS 'KHYAMS PAR GYUR PA'I SEMS CAN RNAMS LA LAS KYI RNAM PAR SMIN
PA MNGON SUM DU BSTAN PA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS DKA'
BA SPYOD PA STON PA DANG, KUN

NAS NYON MONGS PA'I 'JIG RTEN GYI KHAMS 'BYAMS KLAS PAR CHOS NYID
RJES SU 'BRANG BAR BYA BA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS
DKA' BA SPYOD PA STON PA DANG, BDAG GI

DUB PA NYE BAR ZHI ZHING MTHU DANG LDAN PA YONGS SU BSTAN PA'I
PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS DKA' BA SPYOD PA STON PA DANG,
MA YIN NA CHOS LA CHAGS PA RNAMS KYI DON DU

BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS DKA' BA SPYOD PA STON PA DANG, 'DOD
PA'I BDE BA DANG PHRAD PAR BRTZON ZHING RANG GI BDE BA LHUR LEN
PA'I SEMS CAN RNAMS SKYO BAR BYA BA'I PHYIR,

BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS DKA' BA SPYOD PA STON PA DANG, BYANG
CHUB SEMS DPA'I SPYOD PA BRTZAMS PA'I KHYAD PAR YONGS SU BSTAN
PA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS

DKA' BA SPYOD PA STON PA DANG, SKYE BO PHYI MA RNAMS BRTZON 'GRUS
RTZOM PA LA YANG DAG PAR SBYAR BA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'
RNAMS DKA' BA SPYOD PA STON PA DANG, MA YIN


@369B NA DBANG PO YONGS SU MA SMIN PA'I LHA DANG MI RNAMS YONGS
SU SMIN PAR BYA BA'I DUS BSDAD PA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'
RNAMS DKA' BA SPYOD PA STON PA'O, ,KYE RGYAL BA'I SRAS, BCU PO DE
DAG NI, BYANG

CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS SEMS CAN 'DUL BA'I DBANG GI PHYIR, DKA' BA
SPYOD PA'I SBYOR BA YONGS SU STON PA DAG GO, KYE RGYAL BA'I SRAS,
BCU PO 'DI DAG NI, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS KYI SNYING

PO BYANG CHUB TU 'GRO BA STE, BCU GANG ZHE NA, 'DI LTAR 'JIG RTEN
GYI KHAMS THAMS CAD SNANG BAR BYA BA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS
DPA' RNAMS SNYING PO BYANG CHUB TU 'DOD PA DANG, 'JIG RTEN GYI
KHAMS

THAMS CAD RAB TU BSKYOD PA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS
SNYING PO BYANG CHUB TU 'DONG BA DANG, 'JIG RTEN GYI KHAMS THAMS
CAD DU BDAG GI LUS RNAM PAR PHYE BA YONGS SU BSTAN PA'I PHYIR,

BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS SNYING PO BYANG CHUB TU 'DOD PA DANG,
SNGON LHAN CIG TU SPYOD SPYOD PA'I GROGS KYI BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'
RNAMS BSKUL BA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS SNYING

PO BYANG CHUB TU 'DONG BA DANG, SNYING PO BYANG CHUB KYI RGYAN
RNAM PAR PHYE BA YONGS SU BSTAN PA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'
RNAMS SNYING PO BYANG CHUB TU 'DONG BA DANG, SEMS CAN JI LTAR MOS
PA

RNAMS LA LUS DANG, SPYOD LAM DANG, BYANG CHUB KYI SHING GI RGYAN
RNAM PAR PHYE BA YONGS SU BSTAN PA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'
RNAMS SNYING PO BYANG CHUB TU 'DONG BA DANG, 'JIG RTEN GYI KHAMS

MNGON DU BLTA BA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS SNYING PO
BYANG CHUB TU 'DONG BA DANG, GOM PA DOR BA

'JUG CING, SKAD CIG SKAD CIG TU RNAM PAR 'TSANG RGYA BA LAS MI
'DA' BA'I PHYIR, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS SNYING PO BYANG

LTO 'PHYE CHEN PO DANG, BRGYA BYIN DANG, TSANGS PA DANG, 'JIG
RTEN

SEMS DPA' RNAMS SNYING PO BYANG CHUB TU 'DONG BA DANG, CHAGS PA
MED PA'I YE SHES CHEN POS RNAM PAR PHYE BA'I BYANG CHUB
